assistant
```python
import random
import numpy as np

# Define the parameters for synthetic patient data
num_patients = 100
max_age = 100
max_days = 365
max_stage = 4
max_bilirubin = 20
max_albumin = 5
max_cholesterol = 300
max_copper = 300
max_alk_phos = 500
max_sgot = 500
max_triglycerides = 300
max_platelets = 1000
max_prothrombin = 100

# Generate synthetic patient records
patient_records = []
for _ in range(num_patients):
    # Generate random patient data
    id = random.randint(1, 1000)
    days = random.randint(1, max_days)
    status = 'C' if random.random() < 0.7 else 'CL' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'D'
    drug = 'D-penicillamine' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'Placebo'
    age = random.randint(1, max_age)
    sex = 'F' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'M'
    ascites = 'Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N'
    hepatomegaly = 'Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N'
    spiders = 'Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N'
    edema = 'Y' if random.random() < 0.7 else 'S' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N'
    bilirubin = random.randint(0, max_bilirubin)
    cholesterol = random.randint(0, max_cholesterol)
    albumin = random.randint(0, max_albumin)
    copper = random.randint(0, max_copper)
    alk_phos = random.randint(0, max_alk_phos)
    sgot = random.randint(0, max_sgot)
    triglycerides = random.randint(0, max_triglycerides)
    platelets = random.randint(0, max_platelets)
    prothrombin = random.randint(0, max_prothrombin)
    stage = random.randint(1, max_stage)

    # Append the patient record to the list
    patient_records.append({
        'ID': id,
        'N_Days': days,
        'Status': status,
        'Drug': drug,
        'Age': age,
        'Sex': sex,
        'Ascites': ascites,
        'Hepatomegaly': hepatomegaly,
        'Spiders': spiders,
        'Edema': edema,
        'Bilirubin': bilirubin,
        'Cholesterol': cholesterol,
        'Albumin': albumin,
        'Copper': copper,
        'Alk_Phos': alk_phos,
        'SGOT': sgot,
        'Tryglicerides': triglycerides,
        'Platelets': platelets,
        'Prothrombin': prothrombin,
        'Stage': stage
    })

# Convert the list of patient records to a DataFrame
import pandas as pd
df = pd.DataFrame(patient_records)

# Display the first few records
df.head()
```

```python
import random

def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generate random values within medically reasonable ranges
        age = random.randint(18, 80)
        sex = random.choice(['F', 'M'])
        bilirubin = random.uniform(0, 20)
        albumin = random.uniform(0, 5)
        copper = random.uniform(0, 5)
        alk_phos = random.randint(20, 500)
        sgot = random.randint(20, 500)
        tryglicerides = random.uniform(0, 5)
        platelets = random.randint(10, 500)
        prothrombin = random.uniform(10, 20)
        stage = random.randint(1, 4)
        
        # Apply rules to generate realistic data
        if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
            ascites = 'Y'
            edema = 'Y'
        else:
            ascites = 'N'
            edema = 'N'
        
        if stage == 4:
            ascites = 'Y'
            edema = 'Y'
        
        if platelets < 150 and sgot > 100:
            pass  # These conditions are not mutually exclusive, so no action needed
        
        drug = random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'])
        
        record = [
            random.randint(1, 10000),  # ID
            random.randint(1, 365),  # N_Days
            random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D']),  # Status
            drug,
            age,
            sex,
            ascites,
            'Y',  # Hepatomegaly (always present in cirrhosis)
            'Y',  # Spiders (always present in cirrhosis)
            edema,
            bilirubin,
            random.randint(50, 300),  # Cholesterol
            albumin,
            copper,
            alk_phos,
            sgot,
            tryglicerides,
            platelets,
            prothrombin * 1000,  # Convert to seconds
            stage
        ]
        records.append(','.join(map(str, record)))
    
    return records

# Generate 10 records for demonstration
generate_cirrhosis_records(10)
```

import numpy as np
import random

# Define the range for each feature
age_range = (20, 70)  # Age range in days
bilirubin_range = (0, 20)  # Bilirubin range in mg/dL
albumin_range = (1, 5)  # Albumin range in g/dL
copper_range = (0, 4)  # Copper range in µg/dL
alk_phos_range = (20, 200)  # Alkaline phosphatase range in U/L
sgot_range = (20, 500)  # SGOT range in U/L
tryglicerides_range = (20, 500)  # Tryglicerides range in mg/dL
platelets_range = (50, 500)  # Platelets range in ×1000/mm³
prothrombin_range = (10, 20)  # Prothrombin range in seconds

# Define the stages
stages = ['Stage 1', 'Stage 2', 'Stage 3', 'Stage 4']

# Generate synthetic data
data = pd.DataFrame(columns=['ID', 'N_Days', 'Status', 'Drug', 'Age', 'Sex', 'Ascites', 'Hepatomegaly', 'Spiders', 'Edema', 'Bilirubin', 'Cholesterol', 'Albumin', 'Copper', 'Alk_Phos', 'SGOT', 'Tryglicerides', 'Platelets', 'Prothrombin', 'Stage'])

for i in range(100):
    # Generate patient ID
    patient_id = f'ID_{i+1}'
    
    # Generate number of follow-up days

        ascites = 'Y'
    else:
        ascites = 'N'
    
    if random.random() < 0.1:  # 10% chance
        hepatomegaly = 'Y'
    else:
        hepatomegaly = 'N'
    
    if random.random() < 0.1:  # 10% chance
        spiders = 'Y'
    else:
        spiders = 'N'
    
    if random.random() < 0.2:  # 20% chance
        edema = 'Y'
    else:
        edema = 'N'
    
    bilirubin = random.randint(*bilirubin_range)
    cholesterol = random.randint(100, 600)
    albumin = random.uniform(*albumin_range)
    copper = random.uniform(*copper_range)
    alk_phos = random.randint(*alk_phos_range)
    sgot = random.randint(*sgot_range)
    tryglicerides = random.randint(*tryglicerides_range)
    platelets = random.randint(*platelets_range)
    prothrombin = random.uniform(*prothrombin_range)
    
    # Determine stage based on bilirubin and albumin
    if bilirubin > 10.0 and albumin < 2.5:
        stage = 'Stage 4'
    else:
        stage = random.choice

```python
import random

# Parameters
n_records = 50
min_age = 40
max_age = 70
min_days = 30
max_days = 360
min_stage = 1
max_stage = 4
min_bilirubin = 10.0
max_bilirubin = 20.0
min_albumin = 1.0
max_albumin = 2.5
min_cholesterol = 150
max_cholesterol = 300
min_alk_phos = 100
max_alk_phos = 500
min_sgot = 100
max_sgot = 1000
min_platelets = 50
max_platelets = 500
min_copper = 100
max_copper = 200
min_triglycerides = 50
max_triglycerides = 1000
min_prothrombin = 70
max_prothrombin = 140
drugs = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']

# Generate synthetic patient records
data = {
    'ID': range(n_records),
    'N_Days': [random.randint(min_days, max_days) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Status': ['C' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'CL' if random.random() < 0.2 else 'D' for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Drug': [random.choice(drugs) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Age': [random.randint(min_age, max_age) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Sex': ['M' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'F' for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Ascites': ['Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N' for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Hepatomegaly': ['Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N' for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Spiders': ['Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N' for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Edema': ['Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'S' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N' for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Bilirubin': [random.uniform(min_bilirubin, max_bilirubin) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Cholesterol': [random.uniform(min_cholesterol, max_cholesterol) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Albumin': [random.uniform(min_albumin, max_albumin) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Copper': [random.uniform(min_copper, max_copper) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Alk_Phos': [random.uniform(min_alk_phos, max_alk_phos) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'SGOT': [random.uniform(min_sgot, max_sgot) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Tryglicerides': [random.uniform(min_triglycerides, max_triglycerides) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Platelets': [random.uniform(min_platelets, max_platelets) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Prothrombin': [random.uniform(min_prothrombin, max_prothrombin) for _ in range(n_records)],
    'Stage': [random.randint(min_stage, max_stage) for _ in range(n_records)]
}

df = pd.DataFrame(data)
df
```

import random
import numpy as np

# Define the parameters for generating synthetic patient records
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=100):
    # Parameters for generating synthetic data
    age_mean = 55
    age_std = 10
    albumin_mean = 2.5
    albumin_std = 0.5
    bilirubin_mean = 12.0
    bilirubin_std = 3.0
    cholesterol_mean = 200
    cholesterol_std = 50
    copper_mean = 100
    copper_std = 25
    edema_mean = 2
    edema_std = 1
    edema_values = ['N', 'S', 'Y']
    hepatomegaly_mean = 1.5
    hepatomegaly_std = 0.5
    hepatomegaly_values = ['Y', 'N']
    prothrombin_mean = 13.0
    prothrombin_std = 1.0
    prothrombin_values = [12.0, 12.5, 13.0, 13.5, 14.0]
    sgot_mean = 150
    sgot_std = 50
    stage_values = [1, 2, 3, 4]
    
    records = []
    
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generate random values for each feature within medically reasonable ranges
        age = round(random.gauss(age_mean, age_std))
        sex = 'M' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'F'
        bilirubin = round(random.gauss(bilirubin_mean, bilirubin_std))
        albumin = round(random.gauss(albumin_mean, albumin_std))
        cholesterol = round(random.gauss(cholesterol_mean, cholesterol_std))
        copper = round(random.gauss(copper_mean, copper_std))
        alk_phos = round(random.gauss(alk_phos_mean, alk_phos_std))
        sgot = round(random.gauss(sgot_mean, sgot_std))
        tryglicerides = round(random.gauss(tryglicerides_mean, tryglicerides_std))
        platelets = random.randint(100, 500)
        prothrombin = round(random.gauss(prothrombin_mean, prothrombin_std))
        stage = random.choice(stage_values)
        
        # Apply rules to determine the presence of specific symptoms and conditions
        ascites = 'Y' if stage > 2 else 'N'
        hepatomegaly = random.choice(hepatomegaly_values)
        spiders = 'Y' if stage > 2 else 'N'
        edema = random.choice(edema_values)
        
        # Assign the treatment type randomly
        drug = 'D-penicillamine' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'Placebo'
        
        # Determine the status of the patient based on the stage
        if stage == 4:
            status = 'CL'  # Transplant
        elif stage == 3:
            status = 'D'  # Death
        else:
            status = 'C'  # Censored
        
        # Append the generated record to the list
        records.append(
            f"{random.randint(1, 1000)}, "
            f"{random.randint(30, 365)}, "
            f"{status}, "
            f"{drug}, "
            f"{age}, "
            f"{sex}, "
            f"{ascites}, "
            f"{hepatomegaly}, "
            f"{spiders}, "

```python
import random
import numpy as np

# Define the possible values for each feature
ID = np.random.randint(1, 1000)
N_Days = np.random.randint(30, 500)

Drug = ["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"]  # Randomly assign drug
Age = np.random.randint(18, 80)  # Age in days
Sex = ["F", "M"]  # Randomly assign sex
Ascites = ["Y", "N"]
Hepatomegaly = ["Y", "N"]
Spiders = ["Y", "N"]
Edema = ["N", "S", "Y"]  # Randomly assign edema
Bilirubin = np.random.normal(0.5, 1.5)  # Normal distribution around 1
Cholesterol = np.random.normal(150, 30)  # Normal distribution around 150
Albumin = np.random.normal(3.5, 0.5)  # Normal distribution around 3.5
Copper = np.random.normal(90, 10)  # Normal distribution around 90
Alk_Phos = np.random.normal(30, 10)  # Normal distribution around 30
SGOT = np.random.normal(40, 15)  # Normal distribution around 40
Tryglicerides = np.random.normal(60, 10)  # Normal distribution around 60
Platelets = np.random.normal(200, 50)  # Normal distribution around 200
Prothrombin = np.random.normal(11, 1)  # Normal distribution around 11
Stage = np.random.randint(1, 5)  # Randomly assign stage

# Create the patient records
patient_records = list(zip(
    ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin,
    Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage
))
```

ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin, Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define the rules for generating synthetic patient records
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Randomly assign values for each feature
        age = np.random.randint(18, 70) # Age in days
        sex = np.random.choice(['F', 'M']) # Sex
        status = np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D']) # Status
        drug = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']) # Drug
        days_since_diagnosis = np.random.randint(1, 365) # Number of follow-up days
        albumin = np.random.uniform(0, 5) # Albumin in g/dL
        bilirubin = np.random.uniform(0, 20) # Bilirubin in mg/dL
        cholesterol = np.random.uniform(0, 600) # Cholesterol in mg/dL
        copper = np.random.uniform(0, 200) # Copper in µg/dL
        alk_phos = np.random.uniform(20, 1000) # Alkaline phosphatase in U/L
        sgot = np.random.uniform(0, 500) # SGOT in U/L
        tryglicerides = np.random.uniform(0, 1500) # Tryglicerides in mg/dL
        platelets = np.random.randint(10, 400) # Platelets in ×1000/mm³
        prothrombin = np.random.uniform(8, 16) # Prothrombin time in seconds
        stage = np.random.randint(1, 5) # Histologic stage
        
        # Apply the rules to assign values for certain features
        if bilirubin > 10 or albumin < 2.5:
            status = 'C'
        if status == 'D':
            edema = np.random.choice(['slight','marked'])
            ascites = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
        else:
            edema = 'N'
            ascites = 'N'
        if platelets < 150 and sgot > 100:
            # No need to apply any additional rules as this condition is already covered by the rule
            pass
        
        # Append the record to the list
        records.append([
            f'ID_{len(records)}', 
            days_since_diagnosis,
            status,
            drug,
            age,
            sex,
            ascites,
            np.random.choice(['Y', 'N']), # Hepatomegaly
            np.random.choice(['Y', 'N']), # Spiders
            edema,
            bilirubin,
            cholesterol,
            albumin,
            copper,
            alk_phos,
            sgot,
            tryglicerides,
            platelets,
            prothrombin,
            stage
        ])
    
    # Convert the list of records to a pandas DataFrame
    df = pd.DataFrame(records, columns=range(20))
    
    return df

# Generate 100 synthetic cirrhosis patient records
df = generate_cirrhosis_records(100)

# Display the first 5 records
df.head()
```

```python
import random

def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=10, num_days_range=(0, 365)):
    # Define ranges for each feature based on medical rules
    age_range = (30, 80)  # Days
    bilirubin_range = (10, 20)  # mg/dL
    albumin_range = (1, 4)  # g/dL
    copper_range = (100, 200)  # µg/dL
    alk_phos_range = (50, 150)  # U/L
    sgot_range = (50, 200)  # U/L
    tryglicerides_range = (50, 300)  # mg/dL
    platelets_range = (50, 500)  # ×1000/mm³
    prothrombin_range = (10, 14)  # seconds
    stage_range = (1, 4)  # histologic stage
    
    records = []
    
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generate random values for each feature within medically reasonable ranges
        patient_id = random.randint(1000, 9999)
        n_days = random.randint(*num_days_range)
        status = random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'])
        drug = random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'])
        age = random.randint(*age_range)
        sex = random.choice(['F', 'M'])
        ascites = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
        hepatomegaly = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
        spiders = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
        edema = random.choice(['slight','marked'])
        bilirubin = random.uniform(*bilirubin_range)
        cholesterol = random.randint(150, 350)  # mg/dL
        albumin = random.uniform(*albumin_range)
        copper = random.randint(*copper_range)  # µg/dL
        alk_phos = random.randint(*alk_phos_range)  # U/L
        sgot = random.randint(*sgot_range)  # U/L
        tryglicerides = random.randint(*tryglicerides_range)  # mg/dL
        platelets = random.randint(*platelets_range)  # ×1000/mm³
        prothrombin = random.uniform(*prothrombin_range)  # seconds
        stage = random.randint(*stage_range)
        
        # Format the record
        record = f"{patient_id}, {n_days}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {tryglicerides}, {platelets}, {prothrombin}, {stage}"
        records.append(record)
    
    return records

records = generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=5)
records
```

```python
import random
import pandas as pd

# Define the rules for generating synthetic data
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=100):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        record = {
            'ID': 'Patient' + str(len(records) + 1),
            'N_Days': random.randint(0, 365),
            'Status': random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D']),
            'Drug': random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']),
            'Age': random.randint(18, 80),
            'Sex': random.choice(['F', 'M']),
            'Ascites': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Hepatomegaly': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Spiders': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Edema': random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y']),
            'Bilirubin': random.randint(0, 20),
            'Cholesterol': random.randint(0, 300),
            'Albumin': random.randint(0, 5),
            'Copper': random.randint(0, 30),
            'Alk_Phos': random.randint(0, 500),
            'SGOT': random.randint(0, 1000),
            'Tryglicerides': random.randint(0, 300),
            'Platelets': random.randint(0, 150),
            'Prothrombin': random.randint(60, 120),
            'Stage': random.randint(1, 4)
        }
        records.append(record)
    
    df = pd.DataFrame(records)
    return df

# Generate 100 synthetic cirrhosis patient records
cirrhosis_records = generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=100)
cirrhosis_records
```

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from random import choice, uniform

# Define the parameters for generating synthetic patient records
def generate_records(num_records=100):
    # Parameters for synthetic data generation
    age_range = (20, 70)  # Age range in days
    albumin_range = (1.0, 4.0)  # Albumin range in g/dL
    bilirubin_range = (0.0, 20.0)  # Bilirubin range in mg/dL
    cholesterol_range = (100.0, 400.0)  # Cholesterol range in mg/dL
    copper_range = (10.0, 250.0)  # Copper range in µg/dL
    alk_phos_range = (30.0, 500.0)  # Alkaline phosphatase range in U/L
    sgot_range = (30.0, 1000.0)  # SGOT range in U/L
    tryglicerides_range = (20.0, 500.0)  # Tryglicerides range in mg/dL
    platelets_range = (50.0, 600.0)  # Platelets range in ×1000/mm³
    prothrombin_range = (7.0, 15.0)  # Prothrombin range in seconds
    stage_range = list(range(1, 5))  # Stage range from 1 to 4

    # Generate synthetic patient records
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generate random patient information
        patient_id = f'P{len(records) + 1}'
        n_days = int(uniform(365, 1095))  # Number of follow-up days between 1 and 3 years
        status = choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'])  # Status: C=censored, CL=transplant, D=death
        drug = choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'])  # Drug type
        age = int(uniform(*age_range))  # Patient's age in days
        sex = choice(['F', 'M'])  # Sex: F or M
        ascites = choice(['Y', 'N'])  # Ascites: Y or N
        hepatomegaly = choice(['Y', 'N'])  # Hepatomegaly: Y or N
        spiders = choice(['Y', 'N'])  # Spider angiomata: Y or N
        edema = choice([choice(['N', 'S']), 'Y'])  # Edema: N=no, S=slight, Y=marked
        bilirubin = uniform(*bilirubin_range)  # Bilirubin in mg/dL
        cholesterol = uniform(*cholesterol_range)  # Cholesterol in mg/dL
        albumin = uniform(*albumin_range)  # Albumin in g/dL
        copper = uniform(*copper_range)  # Copper in µg/dL
        alk_phos = uniform(*alk_phos_range)  # Alkaline phosphatase in U/L
        sgot = uniform(*sgot_range)  # SGOT in U/L
        tryglicerides = uniform(*tryglicerides_range)  # Tryglicerides in mg/dL
        platelets = uniform(*platelets_range) * 1000  # Platelets count in ×1000/mm³
        prothrombin = uniform(*prothrombin_range)  # Prothrombin time in seconds

```python
import random

def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=10):
    rules = {
        'Bilirubin': lambda: random.uniform(0, 20),
        'Albumin': lambda: random.uniform(0, 5),
        'Platelets': lambda: random.randint(50, 500),
        'SGOT': lambda: random.randint(30, 500),
        'Drug': lambda: random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']),
        'Stage': lambda: random.randint(1, 4),
        'Ascites': lambda: random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
        'Hepatomegaly': lambda: random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
        'Spiders': lambda: random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
        'Edema': lambda: random.choice(['slight','marked']),
        'Age': lambda: random.randint(20, 80),
        'Sex': lambda: random.choice(['M', 'F']),
        'Cholesterol': lambda: random.randint(100, 300),
        'Tryglicerides': lambda: random.randint(50, 300),
        'Copper': lambda: random.uniform(0, 5),
        'Alk_Phos': lambda: random.randint(30, 500),
        'Prothrombin': lambda: random.randint(10, 30)
    }
    
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        record = {}
        for key, value_gen in rules.items():
            record[key] = value_gen()
        records.append(','.join(str(record[key]) for key in rules.keys()))
    
    return '\n'.join(records)

generate_cirrhosis_records(5)
```

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import random

# Define the rules and ranges for synthetic data generation
rules = {
    'Age': lambda: np.random.randint(18, 70),
    'Sex': lambda: np.random.choice(['F', 'M']),
    'Bilirubin': lambda: np.random.uniform(0, 25),
    'Albumin': lambda: np.random.uniform(0, 5),
    'Platelets': lambda: np.random.randint(100, 500),
    'SGOT': lambda: np.random.randint(50, 500),
    'Stage': lambda: np.random.randint(1, 5)
}

# Generate synthetic data based on the given rules
data = {
    'ID': np.arange(1, 101),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(30, 365),
    'Status': np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], size=100),
    'Drug': np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], size=100),
    **{key: rules[key]() for key in rules}
}

# Convert the dictionary to a pandas DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame(data)

# Apply the medical rules to filter the data
df = df[(df['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (df['Albumin'] < 2.5)]
df = df[df['Stage'] >= 3]
df = df[df['Stage'] == 4]  # Only keep stage 4 patients
df = df[(df['Edema'] == 'Y') | (df['Ascites'] == 'Y')]
df = df[df['Platelets'] < 150]
df = df[df['SGOT'] > 100]

# Display the final dataset
df
```

def generate_records():

```python
import random

def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    
    for _ in range(num_records):
        record = {
            'ID': random.randint(1, 1000),
            'N_Days': random.randint(30, 365),
            'Status': random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D']),
            'Drug': random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']),
            'Age': random.randint(20, 80),
            'Sex': random.choice(['F', 'M']),
            'Ascites': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Hepatomegaly': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Spiders': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Edema': random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y']),
            'Bilirubin': random.randint(0, 20),
            'Cholesterol': random.randint(100, 400),
            'Albumin': random.randint(0, 5),
            'Copper': random.randint(0, 10),
            'Alk_Phos': random.randint(50, 500),
            'SGOT': random.randint(0, 500),
            'Tryglicerides': random.randint(0, 500),
            'Platelets': random.randint(50, 500),
            'Prothrombin': random.randint(10, 50),
            'Stage': random.randint(1, 4)
        }
        records.append(','.join(str(value) for value in record.values()))
    
    return '\n'.join(records)

generate_cirrhosis_records(10)
```

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from random import choice

# Parameters
num_patients = 100
min_age = 40
max_age = 70
min_days = 0
max_days = 365
valid_genders = ['F', 'M']
drugs = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']
stages = [1, 2, 3, 4]

# Function to generate random value within range
def generate_value(param, param_name, range_min, range_max):
    if param_name == 'Bilirubin' or param_name == 'Albumin':
        return np.random.uniform(range_min, range_max)
    elif param_name == 'Cholesterol':
        return np.random.uniform(range_min, range_max)
    elif param_name == 'Copper':
        return np.random.uniform(range_min, range_max)
    elif param_name == 'Platelets':
        return np.random.uniform(range_min, range_max)
    elif param_name == 'Prothrombin':
        return np.random.uniform(range_min, range_max)
    elif param_name == 'Stage':
        return choice(stages)
    else:
        return choice([True, False])

# Generate synthetic data
data = pd.DataFrame(columns=['ID', 'N_Days', 'Status', 'Drug', 'Age', 'Sex', 'Ascites', 'Hepatomegaly', 'Spiders', 'Edema', 'Bilirubin', 'Cholesterol', 'Albumin', 'Copper', 'Alk_Phos', 'SGOT', 'Tryglicerides', 'Platelets', 'Prothrombin', 'Stage'])

for i in range(num_patients):
    record = {}
    record['ID'] = i
    record['N_Days'] = np.random.randint(min_days, max_days + 1)
    record['Status'] = choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'])
    record['Drug'] = choice(drugs)
    record['Age'] = np.random.randint(min_age, max_age + 1)
    record['Sex'] = choice(valid_genders)
    record['Ascites'] = generate_value(record['Ascites'], 'Ascites', 0, 1)
    record['Hepatomegaly'] = generate_value(record['Hepatomegaly'], 'Hepatomegaly', 0, 1)
    record['Spiders'] = generate_value(record['Spiders'], 'Spiders', 0, 1)
    record['Edema'] = choice([0, 1, 2, 3])  # 0 = N, 1 = S, 2 = Y
    record['Bilirubin'] = generate_value(record['Bilirubin'], 'Bilirubin', 0, 20)
    record['Cholesterol'] = generate_value(record['Cholesterol'], 'Cholesterol', 100, 400)
    record['Albumin'] = generate_value(record['Albumin'], 'Albumin', 1, 5)
    record['Copper'] = generate_value(record['Copper'], 'Copper', 50, 300)
    record['Alk_Phos'] = generate_value(record['Alk_Phos'], 'Alk_Phos', 20, 200)
    record['SGOT'] = generate_value(record['SGOT'], 'SGOT', 20, 100)
    record['Tryglicerides'] = generate_value(record['Tryglicerides'], 'Tryglicerides', 20, 300)
    record['Platelets'] = generate_value(record['Platelets'], 'Platelets', 50, 600)

```python
import random
import string

# Function to generate a random string of specified length
def random_string(length):
    letters = string.ascii_lowercase
    return ''.join(random.choice(letters) for _ in range(length))

# Function to generate realistic patient records for liver cirrhosis research
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        record = {
            'ID': random_string(10),
            'N_Days': random.randint(1, 365),
            'Status': random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D']),
            'Drug': random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']),
            'Age': random.randint(18, 80),
            'Sex': random.choice(['F', 'M']),
            'Ascites': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Hepatomegaly': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Spiders': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Edema': random.choice(['slight','marked']),
            'Bilirubin': random.randint(1, 20),
            'Cholesterol': random.randint(100, 300),
            'Albumin': random.randint(1, 5),
            'Copper': random.randint(10, 30),
            'Alk_Phos': random.randint(50, 200),
            'SGOT': random.randint(50, 300),
            'Tryglicerides': random.randint(50, 500),
            'Platelets': random.randint(50, 500),
            'Prothrombin': random.randint(10, 30),
            'Stage': random.randint(1, 4)
        }
        records.append(','.join(str(record[key]) for key in record.keys()))
    return '\n'.join(records)

# Generate 10 cirrhosis patient records
generate_cirrhosis_records(10)
```

```python
import random
import numpy as np

# Define the parameters
total_patients = 100
max_age = 70  # in days
max_bilirubin = 20  # mg/dL
max_albumin = 5  # g/dL
max_alk_phos = 300  # U/L
max_chol = 400  # mg/dL
max_copper = 200  # µg/dL
max_platelets = 400  # ×1000/mm³
max_prothrombin = 20  # seconds
max_stage = 4  # histologic stage
max_triglycerides = 300  # mg/dL

# Generate synthetic patient records
patient_records = []
for _ in range(total_patients):
    # Random patient attributes
    age = random.randint(1, max_age)
    sex = random.choice(['F', 'M'])
    bilirubin = random.uniform(0, max_bilirubin)
    albumin = random.uniform(0, max_albumin)
    alk_phos = random.uniform(0, max_alk_phos)
    cholesterol = random.uniform(0, max_chol)
    copper = random.uniform(0, max_copper)
    sgot = random.uniform(0, max_alk_phos)  # Same as alkaline phosphatase for simplicity
    triglycerides = random.uniform(0, max_triglycerides)
    platelets = random.uniform(0, max_platelets)
    prothrombin = random.uniform(0, max_prothrombin)
    stage = random.randint(1, max_stage)

    # Apply medical rules
    ascites = 'Y' if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5 else 'N'
    hepatomegaly = 'Y' if random.random() < 0.7 else 'N'
    spiders = 'Y' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'N'
    edema = random.choice(['slight','marked'])  # 'Y' for marked, 'S' for slight
    if stage == 4:
        edema ='marked'

    # Random status and drug
    status = random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'])
    drug = 'D-penicillamine' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'Placebo'

    # Append the record
    patient_records.append(
        f'{random.randint(1000, 9999)}'
        f', {random.randint(1, 365)}'
        f', {status}'
        f', {drug}'
        f', {age}'
        f', {sex}'
        f', {ascites}'
        f', {hepatomegaly}'
        f', {spiders}'
        f', {edema}'
        f', {bilirubin:.1f}'
        f', {cholesterol:.1f}'
        f', {albumin:.1f}'
        f', {copper:.1f}'
        f', {alk_phos:.1f}'
        f', {sgot:.1f}'
        f', {triglycerides:.1f}'
        f', {platelets:.1f}'
        f', {prothrombin:.1f}'
        f', {stage}'
    )

# Display the first few records
patient_records[:10]

```

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Parameters
num_patients = 100
num_follow_up_days = 365
max_age = 70
min_age = 18
max_bilirubin = 20
min_bilirubin = 1
max_albumin = 4
min_albumin = 0.5
max_alk_phos = 200
min_alk_phos = 30
max_cholesterol = 300
min_cholesterol = 100
max_copper = 200
min_copper = 5
max_edema = 'Y'
min_edema = 'N'
max_hepatomegaly = 'Y'
min_hepatomegaly = 'N'
max_spiders = 'Y'
min_spiders = 'N'
max_stage = 4
min_stage = 1
max_platelets = 500
min_platelets = 50
max_prothrombin = 20
min_prothrombin = 10
max_sgot = 500
min_sgot = 10
max_tryglicerides = 500
min_tryglicerides = 50
max_status = 'C'
min_status = 'C'
max_drug = 'D-penicillamine'
min_drug = 'D-penicillamine'

# Random Seed
np.random.seed(42)

# Generate synthetic patient records
data = {
    'ID': np.random.randint(1, 1000, num_patients),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(0, num_follow_up_days, num_patients),
    'Status': np.random.choice([min_status, max_status], num_patients),
    'Drug': np.random.choice([min_drug, max_drug], num_patients),
    'Age': np.random.randint(min_age, max_age, num_patients),
    'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], num_patients),
    'Ascites': np.random.choice([min_edema, max_edema], num_patients),
    'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice([min_hepatomegaly, max_hepatomegaly], num_patients),
    'Spiders': np.random.choice([min_spiders, max_spiders], num_patients),
    'Edema': np.random.choice([min_edema, max_edema], num_patients),
    'Bilirubin': np.random.randint(min_bilirubin, max_bilirubin, num_patients),
    'Cholesterol': np.random.randint(min_cholesterol, max_cholesterol, num_patients),
    'Albumin': np.random.uniform(min_albumin, max_albumin, num_patients),
    'Copper': np.random.uniform(min_copper, max_copper, num_patients),
    'Alk_Phos': np.random.randint(min_alk_phos, max_alk_phos, num_patients),
    'SGOT': np.random.randint(min_sgot, max_sgot, num_patients),
    'Tryglicerides': np.random.randint(min_tryglicerides, max_tryglicerides, num_patients),
    'Platelets': np.random.randint(min_platelets, max_platelets, num_patients),
    'Prothrombin': np.random.uniform(min_prothrombin, max_prothrombin, num_patients),
    'Stage': np.random.randint(min_stage, max_stage, num_patients),
}

# Create DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame(data)

# Display first few records
df.head()
```

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define the parameters for generating synthetic data
N_patients = 100
N_Days = 365
ages = np.random.normal(50, 10, N_patients)  # Age range: 40-70 years
sexes = np.random.choice(['M', 'F'], N_patients)  # 50% male, 50% female
drugs = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], N_patients)  # 50% D-penicillamine, 50% Placebo
stages = np.random.randint(1, 5, N_patients)  # Stage 1-4

# Generate synthetic patient records
data = {
    'ID': np.arange(1, N_patients+1),
    'N_Days': N_Days,
    'Status': np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], N_patients),  # 50% censored, 25% transplant, 25% death
    'Drug': drugs,
    'Age': ages,
    'Sex': sexes,
    'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], N_patients),
    'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], N_patients),
    'Spiders': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], N_patients),
    'Edema': np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], N_patients),  # 25% no, 50% slight, 25% marked
    'Bilirubin': np.random.normal(6, 2, N_patients),  # Normal range: 0-1.1 mg/dL
    'Cholesterol': np.random.normal(200, 30, N_patients),  # Normal range: 130-199 mg/dL
    'Albumin': np.random.normal(4, 0.5, N_patients),  # Normal range: 3.5-5.0 g/dL
    'Copper': np.random.normal(90, 10, N_patients),  # Normal range: 70-140 µg/dL
    'Alk_Phos': np.random.normal(40, 10, N_patients),  # Normal range: 30-110 U/L
    'SGOT': np.random.normal(30, 10, N_patients),  # Normal range: 8-40 U/L
    'Tryglicerides': np.random.normal(100, 20, N_patients),  # Normal range: 35-140 mg/dL
    'Platelets': np.random.normal(300, 50, N_patients),  # Normal range: 150-450 ×1000/mm³
    'Prothrombin': np.random.normal(12, 0.5, N_patients),  # Normal range: 11-14 seconds
    'Stage': stages
}

# Create a DataFrame from the dictionary
df = pd.DataFrame(data)

# Display the first few records
df.head()
```

```python
import pandas as pd
import random
import numpy as np

# Define the number of records to generate
num_records = 50

# Define the possible values for each feature
values = {
    'ID': range(1, num_records + 1),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(30, 360),
    'Status': ['C', 'CL', 'D'] * (num_records // 3),
    'Drug': ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'] * num_records,
    'Age': np.random.randint(30, 80),
    'Sex': ['F', 'M'] * num_records,
    'Ascites': ['Y', 'N'] * num_records,
    'Hepatomegaly': ['Y', 'N'] * num_records,
    'Spiders': ['Y', 'N'] * num_records,
    'Edema': ['N', 'S', 'Y'] * num_records,
    'Bilirubin': np.random.uniform(0, 20),
    'Cholesterol': np.random.randint(100, 600),
    'Albumin': np.random.uniform(0, 6),
    'Copper': np.random.uniform(0, 3),
    'Alk_Phos': np.random.randint(100, 1000),
    'SGOT': np.random.randint(100, 500),
    'Tryglicerides': np.random.randint(50, 600),
    'Platelets': np.random.randint(50, 500),
    'Prothrombin': np.random.uniform(10, 15),
    'Stage': np.random.randint(1, 5)
}

# Create a DataFrame with the generated data
data = pd.DataFrame(values)

# Generate realistic patient records based on the given medical rules
data.loc[data['Bilirubin'] > 10 | data['Albumin'] < 2.5, 'Stage'] = np.where((data['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (data['Albumin'] < 2.5), 3, data['Stage'])
data.loc[data['Stage'] == 4, ['Ascites', 'Edema']] = 'Y'
data.loc[data['Stage'] == 4, ['Hepatomegaly', 'Spiders']] = 'Y'
data.loc[data['Platelets'] < 150, 'Stage'] = np.where(data['Platelets'] < 150, 4, data['Stage'])
data.loc[data['SGOT'] > 100, 'Stage'] = np.where(data['SGOT'] > 100, 4, data['Stage'])

# Convert the DataFrame to the desired format
records = data[['ID', 'N_Days', 'Status', 'Drug', 'Age', 'Sex', 'Ascites', 'Hepatomegaly', 'Spiders', 'Edema', 'Bilirubin', 'Cholesterol', 'Albumin', 'Copper', 'Alk_Phos', 'SGOT', 'Tryglicerides', 'Platelets', 'Prothrombin', 'Stage']]

# Display the first few records
records.head()
```

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define the parameters for generating the synthetic data
num_patients = 100
max_age = 10000  # Maximum age in days
max_bilirubin = 20  # Maximum bilirubin level in mg/dL
max_cholesterol = 400  # Maximum cholesterol level in mg/dL
max_albumin = 5  # Maximum albumin level in g/dL
max_copper = 250  # Maximum copper level in µg/dL
max_alk_phos = 300  # Maximum alkaline phosphatase level in U/L
max_sgot = 500  # Maximum SGOT level in U/L
max_triglycerides = 2000  # Maximum triglyceride level in mg/dL
max_platelets = 1000  # Maximum platelets count in ×1000/mm³
max_prothrombin = 120  # Maximum prothrombin time in seconds
max_stage = 4  # Maximum histologic stage

# Generate synthetic patient records
data = {
    'ID': np.arange(num_patients),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(1, 500),  # Random number of follow-up days between 1 and 500
    'Status': np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], size=num_patients),  # Random status: C (censored), CL (transplant), D (death)
    'Drug': np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], size=num_patients),  # Random drug: D-penicillamine or Placebo
    'Age': np.random.randint(1, max_age),  # Random age between 1 and max_age
    'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], size=num_patients),  # Random sex: F (female) or M (male)
    'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=num_patients),  # Random ascites: Y (yes) or N (no)
    'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=num_patients),  # Random hepatomegaly: Y (yes) or N (no)
    'Spiders': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=num_patients),  # Random spider angiomatosis: Y (yes) or N (no)
    'Edema': np.random.choice([['N', 'S', 'Y']], size=num_patients),  # Random edema: N (no), S (slight), Y (marked)
    'Bilirubin': np.random.randint(0, max_bilirubin),  # Random bilirubin level between 0 and max_bilirubin
    'Cholesterol': np.random.randint(0, max_cholesterol),  # Random cholesterol level between 0 and max_cholesterol
    'Albumin': np.random.randint(0, max_albumin),  # Random albumin level between 0 and max_albumin
    'Copper': np.random.randint(0, max_copper),  # Random copper level between 0 and max_copper
    'Alk_Phos': np.random.randint(0, max_alk_phos),  # Random alkaline phosphatase level between 0 and max_alk_phos
    'SGOT': np.random.randint(0, max_sgot),  # Random SGOT level between 0 and max_sgot
    'Tryglicerides': np.random.randint(0, max_triglycerides),  # Random triglyceride level between 0 and max_triglycerides

```python
import random
import pandas as pd

def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=100):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Randomly assign values for each feature
        record = {
            'ID': random.randint(1, 1000),
            'N_Days': random.randint(30, 365),
            'Status': random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D']),
            'Drug': random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']),
            'Age': random.randint(18, 80),
            'Sex': random.choice(['F', 'M']),
            'Ascites': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Hepatomegaly': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Spiders': random.choice(['Y', 'N']),
            'Edema': random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y']),
            'Bilirubin': random.uniform(0, 20),
            'Cholesterol': random.uniform(100, 400),
            'Albumin': random.uniform(0, 5),
            'Copper': random.uniform(0, 3),
            'Alk_Phos': random.randint(50, 500),
            'SGOT': random.randint(50, 500),
            'Tryglicerides': random.uniform(0, 300),
            'Platelets': random.randint(50, 300),
            'Prothrombin': random.uniform(10, 20),
            'Stage': random.randint(1, 4),
        }
        records.append(record)
    
    df = pd.DataFrame(records)
    return df

cirrhosis_records = generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records=10)
cirrhosis_records
```
